                  <foreign lang="ar">أَحَقَّ</foreign>;] <hi rend="ital">he lied:</hi> (Mgh:) <hi rend="ital">he made a false,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">vain, claim</hi> or <hi rend="ital">demand; he claimed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">demanded, for himself that which was not right,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">just.</hi> (Lth, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  See also 1.       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ابطلهُ</foreign> [and vulgarly   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n2785-1" target="بطّلهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n2783"/></foreign>] <hi rend="ital">He made it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">rendered it,</hi> [and <hi rend="ital">he proved it to be,</hi>] <foreign lang="ar">بَاطِل</foreign>, i. e. <hi rend="ital">false, untrue, wrong</hi> or <hi rend="ital">incorrect, fictitious, spurious, unfounded, unsound, vain, unreal, naught, futile, worthless, useless, unprofitable,</hi> (S, * L, K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">devoid of virtue</hi> or <hi rend="ital">efficacy, ineffectual, null, void, of no force,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of no account;</hi> (Msb, TA;) <hi rend="ital">he nullified it, annulled it, abolished it, cancelled it;</hi> whether it was true or false, right or wrong, authentic or spurious, valid or null; (TA;) <hi rend="ital">he made it to go for nothing, as a thing of no account,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">as a thing that had perished</hi> or <hi rend="ital">become lost.</hi> (K.)                   <hi rend="ital">contr. of</hi>
